# Math Problem Tree — Full One-to-One Template Coverage

This tree uses mathematical families as leaves. Difficulty is stored on each source problem independently.

**Coverage:** 2,121 templates for 2,121 numbered corpus records; all source round-trip checks passed.

Each table row maps a corpus item to its own template. The complete placeholder constraints and source bindings are in the JSON/JSONL catalog.

### B09 — Direct proportion: mass, length, cost, and quantity / Прямая пропорциональность величин

**Mapped source templates:** 26  
**Reusable family templates:** 2
